              <div class="section">
               <div class="review" id="review_503825573" itemprop="reviews" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
                <link href="http://www.goodreads.com/review/show/503825573" itemprop="url"/>
                <a class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16356723-asmita-gaikwad" title="Asmita Gaikwad">
                 <img alt="Asmita Gaikwad" src="http://d.gr-assets.com/users/1357979892p2/16356723.jpg"/>
                </a>
                <div class="left bodycol">
                 <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
                  <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/503825573?book_show_action=true" itemprop="publishDate">
                   Jan 12, 2013
                  </a>
                  <a class="user" href="/user/show/16356723-asmita-gaikwad" title="Asmita Gaikwad">
                   Asmita Gaikwad
                  </a>
                  rated it
                  <a class=" staticStars stars_4" title="really liked it">
                   4 of 5 stars
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <span class="readable" id="reviewTextContainer503825573" style="">
                   <span id="freeTextContainer2728709741640966431">
                    Many Lives, Many Masters. Brian. L. Weiss.
                    <br/>
                    United States: Simon and Schuster Inc. 1988. 219 pp.
                    <br/>
                    This book written by Dr. Brian. L. Weiss is based on reincarnation and after death life. It gives you an overview of reincarnation and its various faces. The author tells us about the many lives lived by the main lead-Catherine who worked as a laboratory technician in her present lifetime. The author has beautifully framed in the book all the hypnosis therapies he had with his twenty seven year old pat
                   </span>
                   <span id="freeText2728709741640966431" style="display:none">
                    Many Lives, Many Masters. Brian. L. Weiss.
                    <br/>
                    United States: Simon and Schuster Inc. 1988. 219 pp.
                    <br/>
                    This book written by Dr. Brian. L. Weiss is based on reincarnation and after death life. It gives you an overview of reincarnation and its various faces. The author tells us about the many lives lived by the main lead-Catherine who worked as a laboratory technician in her present lifetime. The author has beautifully framed in the book all the hypnosis therapies he had with his twenty seven year old patient Catherine. And he has carefully detailed Catherines past life experiences she shared with him. According to the author this book is a contribution to the continuing research in the field of parapsychology on- before and after birth life. Apart from the information of the many lives Catherine lived, she told the psychotherapist about the in-between states i.e. the time between her death and next life. She could also pass messages from the spirits or the higher masters which, Dr. Brian Weiss says can be done rarely by anybody. Catherine did possess great powers as she, after a few hypnosis sessions could show psychic abilities. Catherine had come to the psychotherapist Dr. Brian Weiss as she wanted to rise above her phobias, her fears, her anxiety attacks and emotional instability. Catherine was not in any way familiar in her present lifetime to the past life details she gave. This gives a strong opinion that she did not make up any stories or was not having a delusion.
                    <br/>
                    The author Dr. Brian Weiss treated many patients with phobias, depression and emotional instability before Catherine. He treated them with anti-depressants, antibiotics and counseling and sometimes with hypnosis and regression therapy. With Catherine when nothing seemed to work and her condition worsened day by day, week by week, he suggested her to take hypnosis but Catherine was hesitant to go for it earlier though she agreed to it later. In her first session of hypnosis she recalled various traumatic experiences of her present lifetime such as the one at the dentist, one when she was pushed into the swimming pool and was choking and the most harrowing experience at the age of three when her drunken father touched and rubbed her all over her body in a dark room. But her symptoms did not seem to fade away. In one on the session she suddenly went to her past life and began narrating her past life experiences. The doctor was shocked and unprepared for it. It was from here that Catherine recalled her various lifetimes and the traumatic experiences she had in them. These experiences are satisfactorily penned down by the author with appropriate dates and years in which they occurred with Catherine. The key to her symptoms could soon be found and her problems were narrowing with every session. Her each lifetime was framed by the author in the same exact words of Catherine. Dr Weiss was unwilling to put down these experiences on paper as he didnt know where it would take his profession. But one fine day he got an insight and wrote it down. His purpose of writing this book basically was that the knowledge he gained by Catherine and the masters should be shared with the world too. He tried to give some knowledge to all those who do not believe in reincarnation. He believed that the way this book changed his life it would change the lives of millions. The target audience he chose is not a particular group anybody can follow it. As it is written down in a very simple language it is easy to understand too. One doesnt have to knack his brain to understand any part of the book. Though it is simple to read, the author has maintained the originality of the events and Catherines words. He has slightly changed Catherines original identity for secrecy. Dr. Brian Weiss has concluded the book with values worth executing in life. The best part of the Brian Weiss book is- he has enlightened the readers how they shouldnt fear their death but live life in a way that they go to their graves with their heads up high with pride. He has amazingly explained how humans have lived life entirely on greed and excesses of material things which will eventually destroy themselves. He also notifies the psychic abilities developed by him and his wife on their journey to discovering the various aspects of life through Catherine.  He has summarized briefly how this whole four years hypnosis session with Catherine has changed his life and how positive he is become towards life. His optimism gives a wave of positivity to the reader. I dont know about reincarnation but the book has surely taught me about being good to everyone because what you give shall come back to you somehow. If you sow seeds of love, you will bear fruits of love only. It tells us to fear the misdeeds we commit because they will come around us some or the other time. While concluding the author has tried to counsel his readers to lead a good quality path throughout life. Though I do not completely believe in reincarnation I do not accuse the ones who do because it is not who you worship or what you believe in but it is about with what intensity you believe in something that arouses you to live a glowing life in the service of others.
                    <br/>
                    If we talk about reincarnation, the book had no significant effect on me on this ground. Though at times doubts about the existence beyond bodily death blew through my mind, I couldnt gather myself to believe it completely. The book has, but, added a great work on the research in the field of reincarnation and after death existence. The human mind is a vast subject to study. We have yet to discover much much more than we know right know. New discoveries certainly shall face criticism and disapproval. The discovery that Earth is round too had to go through condemnation to finally make it a fact.  So nobody can, at present, say dominantly that after death life exists or it doesnt. Until now, it is a matter of faith than fact.
                    <br/>
                   </span>
                   <a data-text-id="2728709741640966431" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">
                    ...more
                   </a>
                  </span>

                function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked &amp;&amp; exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&amp;name=' + shelf_name + '&amp;a=' + action + '&amp;authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('TmX2uAESqmF252okX1PjDootKbzxd5UN9ERHs1bHwRzchxTiPWnRTyOaO30ALJcKMVEzvskSZgrXhtBcivetTQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&amp;book_id=' + book_id + '&amp;refresh=true' + '&amp;authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('JF1A0GhDJvtGm/j2eC9xiE7TQg5+4i8AvRis10r+xBu2v6KKVDhd1RPmqa8nUAWM9a9YDEaH3Aee2js4ls6oSg==')})
  }

Through compelling profiles of people who knowingly planned the experiences mentioned above, Your Souls Plan shows that suffering is not purposeless, but rather imbued with deep meaning. Working with four gifted mediums, author Robert Schwartz reveals the significance of each persons life plan and allows us a fascinating look into the other side.Each personal story focuses on a specific life challenge, organized by type for easy reference. Accessible both to those familiar with the metaphysical aspects of spirituality and to the general reader, the moving narratives that comprise Your Souls Plan help readers awaken to the reality that they are transcendent, eternal souls. With this stirring book as a guide, feelings of anger, resentment, guilt, and victimization are healed and transformed into acceptance, forgiveness, gratitude, and peace. Robert Schwartz is also the author of Your Souls Gift: The Healing Power of the Life You Planned Before You Were Born, which explores the pre-birth planning of spiritual awakening, miscarriage, abortion, caregiving, abusive relationships, sexuality, incest, adoption, poverty, suicide, rape, and mental illness.        <div class=" clearFloats bigBox" id="aboutAuthor">
        <div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer">
         <h2 class="brownBackground">
          <a href="/author/show/72099.Brian_L_Weiss">
           About Brian L. Weiss
          </a>
         </h2>
        </div>
        <div class="bigBoxBody">
         <div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <a href="/author/show/72099.Brian_L_Weiss">
           <img alt="72099" class="right" src="http://d.gr-assets.com/authors/1287232118p2/72099.jpg"/>
          </a>
          <div class="readable">
           <span id="freeTextContainer16862404391467596760">
            As a traditional psychotherapist, Dr. Brian Weiss was astonished and skeptical when one of his patients began recalling past-life traumas that seemed to hold the key to her recurring nightmares and anxiety attacks. His skepticism was eroded, however, when she began to channel messages from "the space between lives," which contained remarkable revelations about Dr. Weiss's family and his dead son.
           </span>
           <span id="freeText16862404391467596760" style="display:none">
            As a traditional psychotherapist, Dr. Brian Weiss was astonished and skeptical when one of his patients began recalling past-life traumas that seemed to hold the key to her recurring nightmares and anxiety attacks. His skepticism was eroded, however, when she began to channel messages from "the space between lives," which contained remarkable revelations about Dr. Weiss's family and his dead son. Using past-life therapy, he was able to cure the patient and embark on a new, more meaningful phase of his own career.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            A graduate of Columbia University and Yale Medical School, Brian L. Weiss M.D. is Chairman Emeritus of Psychiatry at the Mount Sinai Medical Center in Miami.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            Dr. Weiss maintains a private practice in Miami. In addition, Dr. Weiss conducts national and international seminars and experiential workshops as well as training programs for professionals.
            <br/>
            <br/>
            <em>
             (from the author's webpage)
            </em>
           </span>
           <a data-text-id="16862404391467596760" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">
            ...more
           </a>
          </div>
          <a class="actionLink moreLink" href="/author/show/72099.Brian_L_Weiss">
           More about Brian L. Weiss...
          </a>
          <div class="clear">
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class="bigBoxBottom">
